}\n101\t\n102\t    /// Poll for queued jobs and claim one if available.\n103\t    async fn poll_and_claim(&self) -> Result<()> {\n104\t        // Check if we're at capacity\n105\t        let running = self.running_jobs.read().await;\n106\t        if running.len() >= self.config.max_concurrent_jobs {\n107\t            debug!(\"At capacity ({} jobs), skipping poll\", running.len());\n108\t            return Ok(());\n109\t        }\n110\t        drop(running);\n111\t\n112\t        // Reclaim expired claims first\n113\t        let reclaimed = self.coordinator.reclaim_expired_claims()?;\n114\t should be split into chunks.\n203\t    fn should_chunk(&self, job_type: &JobType, params: &JobParams) -> bool {\n204\t        const DEFAULT_CHUNK_SIZE_BYTES: u64 = 268_435_456; // 256 MiB\n205\t\n206\t        match job_type {\n207\t            JobType::DumpImport => {\n208\t                // Chunk if source size exceeds 2x the default chunk size\n209\t                if let Some(size) = params.source_size_bytes {\n210\t                    size > DEFAULT_CHUNK_SIZE_BYTES * 2\n211\t                } else {\n212\t                    false\n213\t                }\n214\t            }\n215\t            JobType::ReshardBackfill => {\n216\t                // Chunk if old_shards exceeds 32 (configurable threshold)\n217\t                if let Some(old_shards) = }\n225\t\n226\t    /// Split a large job into chunks and enqueue them.\n227\t    async fn split_and_enqueue(\n228\t        &self,\n229\t        claimed: &ClaimedJob,\n230\t        job_type: &JobType,\n231\t        params: &JobParams,\n232\t    ) -> Result<()> {\n233\t        let chunk_size_bytes = self.coordinator.default_chunk_size_bytes();\n234\t\n235\t        let chunks = match           // 1. Fetch the dump data from params.source_url\n240\t                // 2. Use dump_chunking::split_dump_into_chunks to split on NDJSON line boundaries\n241\t                // For now, we create size-based chunks that will be aligned to line boundaries\n242\t                // during actual processing by the worker that processes each chunk\n243\t                let source_size = params.source_size_bytes.unwrap_or(0);\n244\t                if source_size == 0 {\n245\t                    return Err(MiroirError::InvalidRequest(\"source_size_bytes is required for dump import chunking\".into()));\n246\t                }\n247\t\n248\t                // Calculate number of chunks (ceiling division)\n249\t                let total_chunks = ((source_size + chunk_size_bytes - 1) / chunk_size_bytes) as u32;\n250\t\n251\t                (0..total_chunks)\n252\t                    .map(|i| {\n253\t                        let i = i as u64;\n254\t                        let start = i * chunk_size_bytes;\n255\t                        let end = std::cmp::min(start + chunk_size_bytes, source_size);\n256\t                        JobChunk {\n257\t                            index: i as u32,\n258\t                            total: total_chunks,\n259\t                            start: start.to_string(),\n260\t                            end: end.to_string(),\n261\t                            size_bytes: end - start,\n262\t                        }\n263\t                    })\n264\t                    .collect()\n265\t            }\n266\t            JobType::ReshardBackfill => {\n267\t                // Use reshard_chunking to split by shard-id range\n268\t                let old_shards = params.old_shards.unwrap_or(1);\n269\t                let target_shards = params.target_shards.unwrap_or(old_shards * 2);\n270\t                let shards_per_chunk = 32; // Configurable shard count per chunk\n271\t\n272\t                let specs = reshard_chunking::split_reshard_into_chunks(\n273\t                    old_shards,\n274\t                    target_shards,\n275\t                    shards_per_chunk,\n276\t                );\n277\t                reshard_chunking::reshard_specs_to_job_chunks(specs)\n278\t            }\n279\t        };\n280\t\n281\t        info!(\"Splitting job {} into {} chunks\", claimed.id, chunks.len());\n282\t        self.coordinator.split_job_into_chunks(claimed, chunks)?;\n283\t\n284\t        Ok(())\n285\t    }\n286\t\n287\t    /// Process a dump import job.\n288\t    async fn process_dump_import(\n289\t        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n290\t        job_id: &str,\n291\t        params: &JobParams,\n292\t    ) -> Result<()> {\n293\t        info!(\"Processing dump import job {}\", job_id);\n294\t\n295\t        // If this is a chunk job, process the chunk\n296\t        if let chunk.total,\n301\t                chunk.start,\n302\t                chunk.end\n303\t            );\n304\t\n305\t            // Parse chunk boundaries\n306\t            let start_offset: u64 =     .map_err(|_| MiroirError::InvalidRequest(\"invalid chunk end offset\".into()))?;\n310\t\n311\t            // Process the dump import chunk\n312\t            let result = Self::process_dump_chunk(\n313\t                coordinator,\n314\t                job_id,\n315\t                params,\n316\t                start_offset,\n317\t                end_offset,\n318\t            ).await;\n319\t\n320\t            match result {\n321\t                Ok((bytes_processed, docs_routed, last_cursor)) => {\n322\t                    let progress = JobProgress {\n323\t                        bytes_processed,\n324\t                        docs_routed,\n325\t                        last_cursor,\n326\t                        error: None,\n327\t                    };\n328\t                    coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n329\t                    info!(\n330\t                        \"Completed dump chunk {}/{}: {} bytes, {} docs\",\n331\t                        chunk.index, chunk.total, bytes_processed, docs_routed\n332\t                    );\n333\t                }\n334\t                Err(e) => {\n335\t                    let progress = JobProgress {\n336\t                        bytes_processed: start_offset,\n337\t                        docs_routed: 0,\n338\t                        last_cursor: start_offset.to_string(),\n339\t                        error: Some(e.to_string()),\n340\t                    };\n341\t                    coordinator.fail_job(job_id, &progress, e.to_string())?;\n342\t                    return Err(e);\n343\t                }\n344\t            }\n345\t        } else {\n346\t            // Parent job was already split, mark as delegated\n347\t            let progress = JobProgress {\n348\t                bytes_processed: 0,\n349\t                docs_routed: 0,\n350\t                last_cursor: \"delegated\".to_string(),\n351\t                error: None,\n352\t            };\n353\t\n354\t            coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n355\t        }\n356\t\n357\t        info!(\"Completed dump import job {}\", job_id);\n358\t\n359\t        Ok(())\n360\t    }\n361\t\n362\t    /// Process a single dump chunk.\n363\t    ///\n364\t    /// This is a simulation of the full dump import processing. In production,\n365\t    /// this would:\n366\t    /// 1. Fetch dump data from params.source_url with Range header\n367\t    /// 2. Parse NDJSON lines (align to line boundaries)\n368\t    /// 3. Route each document to target shard based on primary_key\n369\t    /// 4. Update progress periodically (heartbeat)\n370\t    /// 5. Handle idempotent resume from last_cursor\n371\t    async fn process_dump_chunk(\n372\t        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n373\t        job_id: &str,\n374\t        params: &JobParams,\n375\t        start_offset: u64,\n376\t        end_offset: u64,\n377\t    ) -> Result<(u64, u64, String)> {\n378\t        use crate::router::shard_for_key;\n379\t        use std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n380\t\n381\t        let chunk_size = end_offset - start_offset;\n382\t        let shard_count = params.shard_count.unwrap_or(64);\n383\t        let primary_key = params.primary_key.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"id\");\n384\t\n385\t        // Simulate processing in batches to allow for progress updates\n386\t        let batch_size = 10_000_000; // 10 MB batches\n387\t        let mut bytes_processed = 0u64;\n388\t        let mut docs_routed = 0u64;\n389\t        let mut last_cursor = start_offset.to_string();\n390\t\n391\t        let start_time = Mode C worker loop for processing chunked background jobs (plan §14.5 Mode C).\n//!\n//! The worker continuously polls for queued jobs, claims them, processes them,\n//! and renews claims. Large jobs are split into chunks; chunk jobs execute\n//! the actual work (dump import, reshard backfill).\n\nuse crate::error::{MiroirError, Result};\nuse crate::mode_c_coordinator::{ClaimedJob, tokio::time::interval;\nuse tracing::{debug, info, warn, error};\n\n/// Mode C worker configuration.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ModeCWorkerConfig {\n    /// Poll interval for claiming new jobs.\n    pub poll_interval_ms: u64,\n    /// Heartbeat interval for renewing claims.\n    pub heartbeat_interval_ms: u64,\n    /// Maximum concurrent jobs per worker.\n    pub max_concurrent_jobs: usize,\n}\n\nimpl Default for ModeCWorkerConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            poll_interval_ms: 1000,      // 1 second\n            heartbeat_interval_ms: 10000, // 10 seconds\n            max_concurrent_jobs: 3,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Mode C worker for processing background jobs.\npub struct ModeCWorker {\n    /// Mode C coordinator.\n    coordinator: ModeCCoordinator,\n    /// Worker configuration.\n    config: ModeCWorkerConfig,\n    /// Currently running jobs.\n    running_jobs: Arc<tokio::sync::RwLock<Vec<RunningJob>>>,\n}\n\n/// A job currently being processed by this worker.\nstruct RunningJob {\n    /// Job ID.\n    id: String,\n    /// Job type.\n    type_: JobType,\n    /// Job parameters.\n    params: JobParams,\n    /// Last config: ModeCWorkerConfig,\n    ) -> Self {\n        let coordinator = ModeCCoordinator::new(task_store, pod_id)\n            .with_claim_ttl_ms(30_000) // 30 seconds\n            .with_heartbeat_interval_ms(config.heartbeat_interval_ms as i64);\n\n        Self {\n            coordinator,\n            config,\n            running_jobs: Arc::new(tokio::sync::RwLock::new(Vec::new())),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Start the worker loop.\n    ///\n    /// This runs continuously, polling for jobs and processing them.\n    pub async fn run(&self) -> Result<()> {\n        info!(\"Starting Mode C worker loop\");\n\n        let mut poll_interval = interval(Duration::from_millis(self.config.poll_interval_ms));\n        let mut heartbeat_interval = interval(Duration::from_millis(self.config.heartbeat_interval_ms));\n\n        loop {\n            tokio::select! {\n                _ = poll_interval.tick() => {\n                    if let Err(e) = self.poll_and_claim().await {\n                        error!(\"Error polling for jobs: {}\", e);\n                    }\n                }\n                _ = heartbeat_interval.tick() => {\n                    if let Err(e) = self.renew_claims().await {\n                        error!(\"Error renewing claims: {}\", e);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Poll for queued jobs and claim one if available.\n    async fn poll_and_claim(&self) -> Result<()> {\n        // Check if we're at capacity\n        let running = self.running_jobs.read().await;\n        if running.len() >= self.config.max_concurrent_jobs {\n            debug!(\"At capacity ({} jobs), skipping poll\", running.len());\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n        drop(running);\n\n        // Reclaim expired claims first\n        let reclaimed = self.coordinator.reclaim_expired_claims()?;\n        if reclaimed > 0 {\n            info!(\"Reclaimed {} expired job claims\", reclaimed);\n        }\n\n        // Try to claim a job\n        let claimed = match self.coordinator.claim_job()? {\n            Some(job) => job,\n            None => return Ok(()), // No jobs available\n        };\n\n        let job_id = claimed.id.clone();\n        let job_type_str = claimed.type_.clone();\n\n        info!(\"Claimed job {} (type: {})\", job_id, job_type_str);\n\n        // Parse job type and parameters\n        let job_type = JobType::from_str(&claimed.type_)\n            .ok_or_else(|| &params).await?;\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n\n        // Spawn a task to process the job\n        let running_job = RunningJob {\n            id: job_id.clone(),\n            type_: job_type,\n            params: params.clone(),\n            last_heartbeat: crate::mode_c_coordinator::now_ms(),\n        };\n\n        {\n            let mut running = self.running_jobs.write().await;\n            running.push(running_job);\n        }\n\n        let coordinator = self.coordinator.clone();\n        let running_jobs = self.running_jobs.clone();\n        let job_id_clone = job_id.clone();\n\n        tokio::spawn(async move {\n            let result = match job_type {\n                JobType::DumpImport => Self::process_dump_import(&coordinator, &job_id_clone, &params).await,\n                JobType::ReshardBackfill => Self::process_reshard_backfill(&coordinator, &job_id_clone, &params).await,\n            };\n\n            // Remove from running jobs\n            {\n                let mut running = running_jobs.write().await;\n                running.retain(|j| j.id != job_id_clone);\n            }\n\n            if let Err(e) = result {\n                error!(\"Job {} failed: {}\", job_id_clone, e);\n                let progress = JobProgress::default();\n                let _ = coordinator.fail_job(&job_id_clone, &progress, e.to_string());\n            }\n        });\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Renew claims for all running jobs.\n    async fn renew_claims(&self) -> Result<()> {\n        let running = self.running_jobs.read().await;\n        let now = crate::mode_c_coordinator::now_ms();\n\n        for job in running.iter() {\n            match self.coordinator.renew_claim(&job.id) {\n                Ok(true) => {\n                    debug!(\"Renewed claim for job {}\", job.id);\n                }\n                Ok(false) => {\n                    warn!(\"Failed to renew claim for job {} -        }\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Check if a job should be split into chunks.\n    fn should_chunk(&self, job_type: &JobType, params: &JobParams) -> bool {\n        const DEFAULT_CHUNK_SIZE_BYTES: u64 = 268_435_456; // 256 MiB\n\n        match job_type {\n            JobType::DumpImport => {\n                // Chunk if source size exceeds 2x the default chunk size\n                if let Some(size) = params.source_size_bytes {\n                    size > DEFAULT_CHUNK_SIZE_BYTES * 2\n                } else {\n                    false\n                }\n            }\n            JobType::ReshardBackfill => {\n                // Chunk if old_shards exceeds 32 (configurable threshold)\n                if let Some(old_shards) = params.old_shards {\n                    old_shards > 32\n                } else {\n                    false\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Split a large job into chunks and enqueue them.\n    async fn split_and_enqueue(\n        &self,\n        claimed: &ClaimedJob,\n        job_type: &JobType,\n        params: &JobParams,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        let chunk_size_bytes = self.coordinator.default_chunk_size_bytes();\n\n        let chunks = match job_type {\n            JobType::DumpImport => {\n                // For dump import, split on byte offset boundaries\n                // In a full implementation, we would:\n                // 1. Fetch the dump data from params.source_url\n                // 2. Use dump_chunking::split_dump_into_chunks to split on NDJSON line boundaries\n                // For now, we create size-based chunks that will be aligned to line boundaries\n                // during actual processing by the worker that processes each chunk\n                let source_size = params.source_size_bytes.unwrap_or(0);\n                if source_size == 0 {\n                    return Err(MiroirError::InvalidRequest(\"source_size_bytes is required for dump import chunking\".into()));\n                }\n\n                // Calculate number of chunks (ceiling division)\n                let total_chunks = ((source_size + chunk_size_bytes - 1) / chunk_size_bytes) as u32;\n\n                (0..total_chunks)\n                    .map(|i| {\n                        let i = i as u64;\n                        let start = i * chunk_size_bytes;\n                        let end = std::cmp::min(start + chunk_size_bytes, source_size);\n                        JobChunk {\n                            index: i as u32,\n                            total: total_chunks,\n                            start: start.to_string(),\n                            end: end.to_string(),\n                            size_bytes: end - start,\n                        }\n                    })\n                    .collect()\n            }\n            JobType::ReshardBackfill => {\n                // Use reshard_chunking to split by shard-id range\n                let old_shards = params.old_shards.unwrap_or(1);\n                let target_shards = params.target_shards.unwrap_or(old_shards * 2);\n                let shards_per_chunk = 32; // Configurable shard count per chunk\n\n                let specs = reshard_chunking::split_reshard_into_chunks(\n                    old_shards,\n                    target_shards,\n                    shards_per_chunk,\n                );\n                reshard_chunking::reshard_specs_to_job_chunks(specs)\n            }\n        };\n\n        info!(\"Splitting job {} into {} chunks\", claimed.id, chunks.len());\n        self.coordinator.split_job_into_chunks(claimed, chunks)?;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Process a dump import job.\n    async fn process_dump_import(\n        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n        job_id: &str,\n        params: &JobParams,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        info!(\"Processing dump import job {}\", job_id);\n\n        // If this is a chunk job, process the chunk\n        if let Some(chunk) = &params.chunk {\n            info!(\n                \"Processing dump chunk {}/{} (offsets          .map_err(|_| MiroirError::InvalidRequest(\"invalid chunk end offset\".into()))?;\n\n            // Process the dump import chunk\n            let result = Self::process_dump_chunk(\n                coordinator,\n                job_id,\n                params,\n                start_offset,\n                end_offset,\n            ).await;\n\n            match result {\n                Ok((bytes_processed, docs_routed, last_cursor)) => {\n                    let progress = JobProgress {\n                        bytes_processed,\n                        docs_routed,\n                        last_cursor,\n                        error: None,\n                    };\n                    coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n                    info!(\n                        \"Completed dump chunk {}/{}: {} bytes, {} docs\",\n                        chunk.index, chunk.total, bytes_processed, docs_routed\n                    );\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    let progress = JobProgress {\n                        bytes_processed: start_offset,\n                        docs_routed: 0,\n                        last_cursor: start_offset.to_string(),\n                        error: Some(e.to_string()),\n                    };\n                    coordinator.fail_job(job_id, &progress, e.to_string())?;\n                    return Err(e);\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Parent job was already split, mark as delegated\n            let progress = JobProgress {\n                bytes_processed: 0,\n                docs_routed: 0,\n                last_cursor: \"delegated\".to_string(),\n                error: None,\n            };\n\n            coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n        }\n\n        info!(\"Completed dump import job {}\", job_id);\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Process a single dump chunk.\n    ///\n    /// This is a simulation of the full dump import processing. In production,\n    /// this would:\n    /// 1. Fetch dump data from params.source_url with Range header\n    /// 2. Parse NDJSON lines (align to line boundaries)\n    /// 3. Route each document to target shard based on primary_key\n    /// 4. Update progress periodically (heartbeat)\n    /// 5. Handle idempotent resume from last_cursor\n    async fn process_dump_chunk(\n        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n        job_id: &str,\n        params: &JobParams,\n        start_offset: u64,\n        end_offset: u64,\n    ) -> Result<(u64, u64, String)> {\n        use crate::router::shard_for_key;\n        use std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n\n        let chunk_size = end_offset - start_offset;\n        let shard_count = params.shard_count.unwrap_or(64);\n        let primary_key = params.primary_key.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"id\");\n\n        // Simulate processing in batches to allow for progress updates\n        let batch_size = 10_000_000; // 10 MB batches\n        let mut bytes_processed = 0u64;\n        let mut docs_routed = 0u64;\n        let mut last_cursor = start_offset.to_string();\n\n        let start_time = Instant::now();\n        let heartbeat_interval = Duration::from_secs(5);\n\n        while bytes_processed < chunk_size {\n            let batch_end = std::cmp::min(bytes_processed + batch_size, chunk_size);\n            let batch_bytes = batch_end - bytes_processed;\n\n            // Simulate processing time based on batch size\n            // In production, this would be actual I/O and processing\n            let simulate_delay = Duration::from_millis((batch_bytes / 1_000_000) * 10);\n            tokio::time::sleep(simulate_delay).await;\n\n            // Simulate document routing\n            // Estimate ~100KB per document (typical JSON document)\n            let estimated_docs = batch_bytes / 100_000;\n            for i in 0..estimated_docs {\n                // Simulate document key\n                let doc_key = format!(\"{}-{}-{}\", primary_key, start_offset + bytes_processed, i);\n                let _shard_id = shard_for_key(&doc_key, shard_count);\n                // In production, we would route the document to the target node/shard\n            }\n\n            bytes_processed = batch_end;\n            docs_routed += estimated_docs;\n            last_cursor = (start_offset + bytes_processed).to_string();\n\n            // Update progress periodically\n            let bytes_processed,\n                    docs_routed,\n                    last_cursor: last_cursor.clone(),\n                    error: None,\n                };\n                coordinator.update_progress(job_id, &progress, crate::mode_c_coordinator::JobState::InProgress)?;\n\n                // Renew the claim\n                let _ = coordinator.renew_claim(job_id);\n\n                // Reset the timer\n                let _ = start_time.elapsed();\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok((bytes_processed, docs_routed, last_cursor))\n    }\n\n    /// Process a reshard backfill job.\n    async fn process_reshard_backfill(\n        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n        job_id: &str,\n        params: &JobParams,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        info!(\"Processing reshard backfill job {}\", job_id);\n\n        // If this is a chunk job, process the shard range\n        if let Some(chunk) = &params.chunk {\n            let (start_shard, end_shard) =     end_shard,\n            ).await;\n\n            match result {\n                Ok((docs_backfilled, last_cursor)) => {\n                    let progress = JobProgress {\n                        bytes_processed: 0, // Not applicable for reshard\n                        docs_routed: docs_backfilled,\n                        last_cursor,\n                        error: None,\n                    };\n                    coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n                    info!(\n                        \"Completed reshard chunk {}/{}: {} docs from shards {}-{}\",\n                        chunk.index, chunk.total, docs_backfilled, start_shard, end_shard\n                    );\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    let progress = JobProgress {\n                        bytes_processed: 0,\n                        docs_routed: 0,\n                        last_cursor: start_shard.to_string(),\n                        error: Some(e.to_string()),\n                    };\n                    coordinator.fail_job(job_id, &progress, e.to_string())?;\n                    return Err(e);\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Parent job was already split, mark as delegated\n            let progress = JobProgress {\n                bytes_processed: 0,\n                docs_routed: 0,\n                last_cursor: \"delegated\".to_string(),\n                error: None,\n            };\n\n            coordinator.complete_job(job_id, &progress)?;\n        }\n\n        info!(\"Completed reshard backfill job {}\", job_id);\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Process a single reshard backfill chunk.\n    ///\n    /// This is a simulation of the full reshard backfill processing. In production,\n    /// this would:\n    /// 1. Read documents from old shard range [start_shard, end_shard)\n    /// 2. Re-route each document to new shard configuration\n    /// 3. Update progress periodically (heartbeat)\n    /// 4. Handle idempotent resume from last_cursor\n    async fn process_reshard_chunk(\n        coordinator: &ModeCCoordinator,\n        job_id: &str,\n        params: &JobParams,\n        start_shard: u32,\n        end_shard: u32,\n    ) -> Result<(u64, String)> {\n        use crate::router::{shard_for_key, assign_shard_in_group};\n        use crate::topology::{Topology, Group, NodeId};\n        use std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n\n        let old_shards = params.old_shards.unwrap_or(64);\n        let target_shards = params.target_shards.unwrap_or(128);\n        let shard_count = (end_shard - start_shard) as u64;\n\n        // Simulate processing in batches to allow for progress updates\n        let batch_shards = 4; // Process 4 shards at a time\n        let mut shards_processed = 0u32;\n        let mut docs_backfilled = 0u64;\n        let mut last_cursor = start_shard.to_string();\n\n        let start_time = Instant::now();\n        let heartbeat_interval = Duration::from_secs(5);\n\n        // Create a simple topology for routing simulation\n        let topology = Topology::new(2, 1, 3); // 2 groups, 1 RF, 3 nodes per group\n\n        while start_shard + shards_processed < end_shard {\n            let batch_end = std::cmp::min(start_shard + shards_processed + batch_shards, end_shard);\n            let batch_count = (batch_end - (start_shard + shards_processed)) as u64;\n\n            // Simulate document processing for each shard\n            // Estimate ~1000 documents per shard\n            for shard_id in (start_shard + shards_processed)..batch_end {\n                let estimated_docs = 1000u64;\n\n                for i in 0..estimated_docs {\n                    // Simulate document key\n                    let doc_key = format!(\"doc-shard{}-{}\", shard_id, i);\n\n                    // Compute old shard assignment\n                    let _old_shard = shard_for_key(&doc_key, old_shards);\n\n                    // Compute new shard assignment\n                    let new_shard = shard_for_key(&doc_key, target_shards);\n\n                    // In production, we would:\n                    // 1. Read the document from the old shard\n                    // 2. Write it to the new shard assignment\n                    // 3. Handle any conflicts or duplicates\n\n                    // Simulate routing to replica groups\n                    for group in topology.groups() {\n                        let _targets = assign_shard_in_group(new_shard, group.nodes(), topology.rf());\n                        // In production, we would write to these target nodes\n                    }\n                }\n\n                docs_backfilled += estimated_docs;\n            }\n\n            shards_processed = batch_end - start_shard;\n            last_cursor = (start_shard + shards_processed as u32).to_string();\n\n            // Update progress periodically\n            let elapsed = start_time.elapsed();\n            if elapsed >= heartbeat_interval {\n                // Update progress and renew claim\n                let progress = JobProgress {\n                    bytes_processed: 0,\n                    docs_routed: docs_backfilled,\n                    last_cursor: last_cursor.clone(),\n                    error: None,\n                };\n                coordinator.update_progress(job_id, &progress, crate::mode_c_coordinator::JobState::InProgress)?;\n\n                // Renew the claim\n                let _ = coordinator.renew_claim(job_id);\n\n                // Reset the timer\n                let _ = start_time.elapsed();\n            }\n\n            // Simulate processing time\n            tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_millis(50)).await;\n        }\n\n        Ok((docs_backfilled, last_cursor))\n    }\n}\n","numLines":610,"startLine":1,"totalLines":610}}}

test_acceptance_1gb_dump_splits_into_4_chunks() {\n    // Acceptance: 1 GB dump: first pod splits into 4× 256 MiB chunks\n    let coord = test_coordinator(\"pod-1\");\n\n    // Enqueue a 1GB dump import job\n    let params = dump_import_params(1_073_741_824); // 1 GiB\n    let job_id = coord.enqueue_job(JobType::DumpImport, params.clone()).unwrap();\n\n    // Claim the job\n    let claimed = coord.claim_job().unwrap().expect(\"should claim job\");\n    assert_eq!(claimed.id, job_id);\n    assert_eq!(claimed.claimed_by, \"pod-1\");\n\n    // Split into chunks (4 chunks of ~256 MiB each)\n    let chunk_size = 268_435_456; // 256 MiB\n    // Ceiling division: (size + chunk_size - 1) / chunk_size\n    let total_chunks = ((1_073_741_824 + chunk_size - 1) / chunk_size) as u32;\n\n    let chunks: Vec<_> = (0..total_chunks)\n        .map(|i| {\n            let i = i as u64;\n            let start = i * chunk_size;\n            let end = std::cmp::min(start + chunk_size, 1_073_741_824u64);\n            crate::mode_c_coordinator::JobChunk {\n                index: i as u32,\n                total: total_chunks,\n                start: start.to_string(),\n assert_eq!(chunk_ids.len(), 4);\n\n    // Verify chunks are queued\n    let child_jobs = coord.list_chunks(&job_id).unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(child_jobs.len(), 4);\n\n    // Verify all chunks are in queued state\n    for child in &child_jobs {\n        assert_eq!(child.state, \"queued\");\n        assert_eq!(child.parent_job_id, Some(job_id.clone()));\n    }\n}\n\n#[test]\nfn test_acceptance_claim_expires_after_30s() {\n    // Acceptance: Kill a claimant mid-chunk: claim expires in 30s;\n    // another pod picks up and resumes at last_cursor\n    let store = Arc::new(SqliteTaskStore::open_in_memory().unwrap());\n    store.migrate().unwrap();\n\n    let coord1 = test_coordinator_with_store(\"pod-1\", store.clone());\n\n    // Enqueue a job\n    let params coord.enqueue_job(JobType::DumpImport, params).unwrap();\n    }\n\n    // Queue depth should be 15\n    assert_eq!(coord.queue_depth().unwrap(), 15);\n\n    // Claim 5 jobs\n    for _ in 0..5 {\n Each chunk can process a range of old shards independently.\n\nuse crate::mode_c_coordinator::{JobChunk, JobParams};\n\n/// Chunk specification for a reshard backfill.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct ReshardChunkSpec {\n    /// Chunk index (0-based).\n    pub index: u32,\n    /// Total number of chunks.\n    pub total: u32,\n    /// Starting old shard ID (inclusive).\n    pub start_shard: u32,\n    /// Ending old shard ID (exclusive).\n    pub end_shard: u32,\n    /// Number of shards in this chunk.\n    pub shard_count: u32,\n}\n\n/// Split a reshard backfill into chunks by shard-id ranges.\n///\n/// Returns a vector of chunk specifications. Each chunk contains a range\n/// of old shards to backfill to the new shard configuration.\n///\n/// # Arguments\n/// * `old_shards` - Number of shards in the old configuration\n/// * `target_shards` - Number of shards in the new configuration\n/// * `shards_per_chunk` - Target number of old shards per chunk\n///\n/// # Returns\n/// A vector of chunk specifications\npub fn split_reshard_into_chunks(\n    old_shards: u32,\n    target_shards: u32,\n    shards_per_chunk: u32,\n) -> Vec<ReshardChunkSpec> {\n    if old_shards == 0 {\n        return Vec::new();\n    }\n\n    // If we have fewer shards than the chunk size, return a single chunk\n    if old_shards <= shards_per_chunk {\n        return vec![ReshardChunkSpec {\n            index: 0,\n            total: 1,\n            start_shard: 0,\n            end_shard: old_shards,\n            shard_count: old_shards,\n        }];\n    }\n\n    let mut chunks = Vec::new();\n    let mut current_shard = 0u32;\n    let mut chunk_index = 0u32;\n\n    while current_shard < old_shards {\n        let end_shard = (current_shard + shards_per_chunk).min(old_shards);\n        let shard_count = end_shard - current_shard;\n\n        chunks.push(ReshardChunkSpec {\n            index: chunk_index,\n            total: 0, // Will be filled in later\n            start_shard: current_shard,\n            end_shard,\n            shard_count,\n        });\n\n        current_shard = end_shard;\n        chunk_index += 1;\n    }\n\n    // Update the total count for all chunks\n    let total = chunks.len() as u32;\n    for chunk in &mut chunks {\n        chunk.total = total;\n    }\n\n    chunks\n}\n\n/// Convert reshard chunk specs to job chunks for the Mode C coordinator.\npub fn reshard_specs_to_job_chunks(specs: Vec<ReshardChunkSpec>) -> Vec<JobChunk> {\n    specs\n        .into_iter()\n        .map(|spec| JobChunk {\n            index: spec.index,\n            total: spec.total,\n            start: spec.start_shard.to_string(),\n            end: spec.end_shard.to_string(),\n            size_bytes: spec.shard_count as u64, // Use shard count as the size metric\n        })\n        .collect()\n}\n\n/// Parse a reshard chunk from a job chunk.\n///\n/// Returns the shard range for the chunk.\npub fn parse_reshard_chunk(chunk: &JobChunk) -> Result<(u32, u32), String> {\n    let start_shard = chunk\n        .start\n        .parse::<u32>()\n        .map_err(|e| format!(\"invalid start shard: {}\", e))?;\n    let end_shard = chunk\n        .end\n        .parse::<u32>()\n        .map_err(|e| format!(\"invalid end shard: {}\", e))?;\n\n    Ok((start_shard, end_shard))\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_zero_old_shards() {\n assert_eq!(chunks[0].end_shard, 16);\n        assert_eq!(chunks[0].shard_count, 16);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_multiple_chunks() {\n        let chunks = split_reshard_into_chunks(64, 128, 0);\n        assert_eq!(chunks[0].end_shard, 16);\n        assert_eq!(chunks[0].shard_count, 16);\n\n        // Verify second chunk\n        assert_eq!(chunks[1].index, 1);\n        assert_eq!(chunks[1].start_shard, 16);\n        assert_eq!(chunks[1].end_shard, 32);\n        assert_eq!(chunks[1].shard_count, 16);\n\n        // Verify last chunk\n        assert_eq!(chunks[3].index, 3);\n        assert_eq!(chunks[3].start_shard, 48);\n        assert_eq!(chunks[3].end_shard, 64);\n        assert_eq!(chunks[3].shard_count, 16);\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_partial_final_chunk() {\n        // 65 shards with 16 per chunk = 4 full chunks + 1 partial\n        let chunks = split_reshard_into_chunks(65, 128, 16);\n        assert_eq!(chunks.len(), 5);\n\n        // First 4 chunks should have 16 shards each\n        for i in 0..4 {\n            assert_eq!(chunks[i].shard_count, 16);\n        }\n\n        // Last chunk should have 1 shard\n
